 - taran adarsh (@taran_adarsh) June 18, 2018 dilli kii ek adaalat ne atirikt 2-ji spectrum aavanton maamle main sunwaayee kii agali taarikh 8 july tay kii he
 Bharti Cellular CMD Sunil Mittal, Essar Group promoter Ravi Ruia and others have been summoned as accused in the case
 sibiai ke vishesh nyaayadhish opi saini ne maamle kii sunwaayee aage taal di kyonki ucchtam nyaayalay ne 26 april ko mittal kii yachika par sibiai ko notice jari kiya tha
 Mittal had challenged the summons issued against him and said that the proceedings in the lower court would be 'postponed' till further orders
 ucchtam nyaayalay ne ruiya or mittal ko nichali adaalat main vyaktigat rup se upasthit hone se chhot de di thi or agency ko jawaab daakhil karne ke liye chaar hafte kaa vakt diya tha
 Mittal was also given three weeks to respond to the cbi's response
 mittal or ruiya sibiai kii vishesh adaalat main aaj upasthit nahin hue jabaki ek anya aaropee enarai aseem ghosh ko abhi tak is maamle main saman jari nahin kiya gaya he
 He was the then Managing Director of the accused company Hutchinson Max Telecom Private Limited
 baharhaal, purv doorsanchaar sachiv shyaamal ghosh aaj adaalat main upasthit hue
 He is also an accused in this case
 do nyaayadhishon ko maamle kii sunwaayee se alag karne ke baad ucchtam nyaayalay ke pradhan nyaayadhish altamas kabir kii adhyakshata vaali nai peeth mittal or ruiya kii yachika par sunwaayee kar rahi he
 Both challenged the summons order of the lower court
 isse pehle mittal or ruiya nichali adaalat ke samaksh upasthit hue the or ucchtam nyaayalay ke aadesh ke mutabik, unhone nijee muchalke bhare the
 On March 19, the special court issued summons to Mittal, Ruia and Aseem Ghosh
 ruiya aaropee companiyon main se ek sterling celular limited ke tatkaaleen nideshak the
 His name was not mentioned in the charge sheet filed by the CBI in the case on December 21 last year
 teenon ke alaava adaalat ne shyaamal ghosh or teen doorsanchaar companiyon bharti celular limited, hachinson maiks telecom praivet limited (ab vodaphone india limited ke naam se prachlit) or sterling celular limited (ab vodaphone mobile sarvice limited ke naam se mashhoor) ko aaropee ke taur par saman bheja tha
 In its charge sheet, the CBI had mentioned the names of the three telecom companies as accused in the additional spectrum allocation case by the Department of Telecommunications, which allegedly caused a loss of Rs 846 crore to the revenue
 ucchtam nyaayalay main sibiai ne jab mittal kii yachika kaa virodh karte hue kaha ki maamle main jaanch ke dauraan unke khilaaf saboot mili hai to ucchtam nyaayalay ne poocha tha ki phir aaropapatr main unke naam kaa zikr kyon nahin he 
 The CBI had on 21 December last year filed a chargesheet against Shyamal Ghosh and three telecom companies Bharti Cellular Limited, Hutchinson Max Telecom Private Limited and Sterling Cellular Limited
 tippaniyan Mittal, Ruia and Aseem Ghosh were not mentioned in the CBI chargesheet as accused, the special court in its order said that they were taking cognizance of the case and issuing summons to all the seven accused including them for April 11
 is 
 vishesh adaalat ne kaha tha ki mittal, ruiya or aseem ghosh ‘‘prathamdrishtya’’ apni
 
 apni companiyon ke ‘‘niyantrankarta’’ hai jinke khilaaf sibiai ne aapraadhik shadyantr kaa aaropapatr daayar kiya he
 Special CBI Judge OP Saini postponed the hearing of the case as the Supreme Court had on April 26 issued notice to the CBI on Mittal's plea
 mittal ne apane khilaaf jari saman ko chunauti di thi or kaha tha ki agle aadesh tak nichali adaalat main kaarywahi ‘sthagit’ rahegi
 The Supreme Court had exempted Ruia and Mittal from appearing in person in the lower court and gave the agency four weeks to file a reply
 mittal ko bhi sibiai ke jawaab par pratikriya ke liye teen hafte kaa vakt diya gaya
 Mittal and Ruia did not appear in the CBI special court today while another accused NRI Aseem Ghosh is yet to be summoned in the case
 vah aaropee company hachinson maiks telecom praivet limited ke tatkaaleen prabandh nideshak the
 However, former Telecom Secretary Shyamal Ghosh appeared in the court today
 vah bhi is maamle main aaropee hai
 After separating the two judges from hearing the case, a new bench headed by Chief Justice Altamas Kabir of the Supreme Court is hearing the petition of Mittal and Ruia
 donon ne nichali adaalat ke saman aadesh ko chunauti di thi
 Earlier, Mittal and Ruia appeared before the trial court and as per the Supreme Court order, they had filed personal bonds
 vishesh adaalat ne 19 march ko mittal, ruiya or aseem ghosh ko saman jari kiya tha
 Ruia was the then director of Sterling Cellular Limited, one of the accused companies
 maamle main pichley varsh 21 disambar ko sibiai dwaara daayar aaropapatr main unke naam kaa zikr nahin tha
 Apart from the three, the court also named Shyamal Ghosh and three telecom companies Bharti Cellular Limited, Hutchinson Max Telecom Private Limited (now popularly known as Vodafone India Limited) and Sterling Cellular Limited (now known as Vodafone Mobile Service Limited) as accused
 Summon was sent sibiai ne apane aaropapatr main doorsanchaar vibhaag dwaara atirikt spectrum aavanton maamle main teenon doorsanchaar companiyon kaa naam aaropee ke rup main zikr kiya tha jisase rajasav ko kathith rup se 846 karod rupaye kaa nuksaan hua tha 
 When the CBI opposed Mittal's plea in the Supreme Court, saying that evidence had been found against him during the investigation in the case, the Supreme Court had asked why his name was not mentioned in the charge sheet
 sibiai ne pichley varsh 21 disambar ko shyaamal ghosh or teen doorsanchaar companiyon bharti celular limited, hachinson maiks telecom praivet limited or sterling celular limited ke khilaaf aaropapatr daayar kiya tha 
 The comments mittal, ruiya or aseem ghosh kaa sibiai ke aaropapatr main aaropee ke rup main zikr nahin tha, vishesh adaalat ne apane aadesh main kaha tha ki vah maamle kaa sangyaan le rahi he or un sahit sabhi saat aropiyon ko 11 april ke liye samman jari kar rahi he 
 The special court had said that Mittal, Ruia and Aseem Ghosh were "prima facie" their own
 
 There are "controllers" of its companies against whom the CBI has filed a charge sheet of criminal conspiracy
